## A weakly-supervised deep learning model for fast localisation and delineation of the skeleton, internal organs, and spinal canal on Whole-Body Diffusion-Weighted MRI (WB-DWI)
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.20722v1
- **Authors**: ['A. Candito', 'A. Dragan', 'R. Holbrey', 'A. Ribeiro', 'R. Donners', 'C. Messiou', 'N. Tunariu', 'D. -M. Koh', 'M. D. Blackledge', 'The Institute of Cancer Research', 'London', 'United Kingdom', 'The Royal Marsden NHS Foundation Trust', 'London', 'United Kingdom', 'University Hospital Basel', 'Basel', 'Switzerland']
- **Abstrat**: Background: Apparent Diffusion Coefficient (ADC) values and Total Diffusion Volume (TDV) from Whole-body diffusion-weighted MRI (WB-DWI) are recognized cancer imaging biomarkers. However, manual disease delineation for ADC and TDV measurements is unfeasible in clinical practice, demanding automation. As a first step, we propose an algorithm to generate fast and reproducible probability maps of the skeleton, adjacent internal organs (liver, spleen, urinary bladder, and kidneys), and spinal canal. Methods: We developed an automated deep-learning pipeline based on a 3D patch-based Residual U-Net architecture that localizes and delineates these anatomical structures on WB-DWI. The algorithm was trained using "soft-labels" (non-binary segmentations) derived from a computationally intensive atlas-based approach. For training and validation, we employed a multi-center WB-DWI dataset comprising 532 scans from patients with Advanced Prostate Cancer (APC) or Multiple Myeloma (MM), with testing on 45 patients. Results: Our weakly-supervised deep learning model achieved an average dice score/precision/recall of 0.66/0.6/0.73 for skeletal delineations, 0.8/0.79/0.81 for internal organs, and 0.85/0.79/0.94 for spinal canal, with surface distances consistently below 3 mm. Relative median ADC and log-transformed volume differences between automated and manual expert-defined full-body delineations were below 10% and 4%, respectively. The computational time for generating probability maps was 12x faster than the atlas-based registration algorithm (25 s vs. 5 min). An experienced radiologist rated the model's accuracy "good" or "excellent" on test datasets. Conclusion: Our model offers fast and reproducible probability maps for localizing and delineating body regions on WB-DWI, enabling ADC and TDV quantification, potentially supporting clinicians in disease staging and treatment response assessment.


**Translated Abstract**: 

背景：表观扩散系数（ADC）值和总扩散体积（TDV）是来自全身扩散加权MRI（WB-DWI）的公认癌症影像生物标志物。然而，手动疾病描绘的ADC和TDV测量在临床实践中不可行，需求自动化。作为第一步，我们提出了一种算法来生成快速和可重复的骨骼、相邻内脏器官（肝脏、脾脏、尿膀胱和肾脏）以及脊髓管的概率图。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文的研究背景是全身扩散加权MRI（WB-DWI）中的表观扩散系数（ADC）和总扩散体积（TDV）被认可为癌症影像生物标志物，但手动描绘无法在临床中实现，需要自动化工具。

- (2): 过去的方法依赖于计算密集型的图谱基础方法，存在手动描绘时间长且不够准确的问题。提出的方法采用基于3D补丁的残差U-Net架构，利用“软标签”进行训练，能够快速且一致地产生概率图，解决了手动方法效率低下的问题。该方法具有很强的动机性。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于提出了一种快速且可重复的深度学习模型，能够在WB-DWI中对骨骼、内脏器官和脊髓管进行定位和描绘，以便于相关生物标志物的量化。

- (4): 本文提出的研究方法是一个自动化的深度学习管道，基于3D补丁的残差U-Net架构，通过重用来自多个中心的532个扫描样本进行训练和验证，以生成所需的概率图。

- (5): 本测方法在定位和描绘任务上，达到的平均Dice分数为0.66（骨骼）、0.8（内脏器官）和0.85（脊髓管），表面距离均低于3mm，表现支持其在疾病分期和治疗反应评估中的应用目标。


## Semantic Communications via Features Identification
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.20720v1
- **Authors**: ['Federico Francesco Luigi Mariani', 'Michele Zhu', 'Maurizio Magarini']
- **Abstrat**: The development of the new generation of wireless technologies (6G) has led to an increased interest in semantic communication. Thanks also to recent developments in artificial intelligence and communication technologies, researchers in this field have defined new communication paradigms that go beyond those of syntactic communication to post-Shannon and semantic communication. However, there is still need to define a clear and practical framework for semantic communication, as well as an effective structure of semantic elements that can be used in it. The aim of this work is to bridge the gap between two post-Shannon communication paradigms, and to define a robust and effective semantic communication strategy that focuses on a dedicated semantic element that can be easily derived from any type of message. Our work will take form as an innovative communication method called identification via semantic features, which aims at exploiting the ambiguities present in semantic messages, allowing for their identification instead of reproducing them bit by bit. Our approach has been tested through numerical simulations using a combination of machine learning and data analysis. The proposed communication method showed promising results, demonstrating a clear and significant gain over traditional syntactic communication paradigms.


**Translated Abstract**:  

随着新一代无线技术（6G）的发展，语义通信的兴趣日益增加。得益于人工智能和通信技术的最新进展，研究人员在这一领域提出了超越语法通信的新的通信范式，包括后香农通信和语义通信。然而，仍然需要为语义通信界定清晰且实用的框架，以及有效的语义元素结构。本文旨在弥合两个后香农通信范式之间的差距，定义一种健壮而有效的语义通信策略，重点关注可从任何类型消息中轻松提取的专用语义元素。我们的工作将形成一种名为通过语义特征识别的创新通信方法，该方法旨在利用语义消息中存在的歧义，以便识别这些消息，而不是逐位重现。我们的方法通过数值仿真进行了测试，结合了机器学习和数据分析。所提出的通信方法显示出良好的结果，相较于传统的语法通信范式具有明确和显著的优势。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文研究背景是新一代无线技术（6G）的发展及语义通信的兴起，旨在解决传统通信方法面临的挑战。

- (2): 过去的方法主要侧重于语法通信和线性消息传输，但在处理语义信息时存在效率低下和灵活性不足的问题。所提出的方法通过传输语义特征而非整体消息，充分利用语义消息中的歧义，从而解决了传输中信息效率低下的问题。提出的方法，尤其是通过语义特征识别，具有良好的动机。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于整合不同的语义通信方法，提出了一个可实用的语义元素结构，并通过数值分析验证其在减少信号传输中比特数方面的有效性。

- (4): 本文研究方法采用了“Teacher-Apprentice”通信框架与消息识别范式相结合，提出了通过语义特征进行识别的新通信方法。

- (5): 所提出的方法在通过数值仿真实验中针对语义元素识别任务取得了显著的性能提升，表明其能够有效支持预期目标。


# AGN
## Explaining the UV to X-ray correlation in AGN within the framework of X-ray illumination of accretion discs
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.20770v1
- **Authors**: ['E. Kammoun', 'I. E. Papadakis', 'M. Dovčiak', 'E. Lusso', 'E. Nardini', 'G. Risaliti']
- **Abstrat**: It is established that the ultraviolet (UV) and X-ray emissions in active galactic nuclei (AGN) are tightly correlated. This correlation is observed both in low- and high-redshift sources. In particular, observations of large samples of quasars revealed the presence of a non-linear correlation between UV and X-rays. The physical origin of this correlation is poorly understood. In this work, we explore this observed correlation in the framework of the X-ray illumination of the accretion disc by a central source. We have shown in previous works that this model successfully explains the continuum UV/optical time delays, variability, and the broadband spectral energy distribution in AGN. We use this model to produce $150,000$ model SEDs assuming a uniform distribution of model parameters. We compute the corresponding UV ($ 2500~\r{A} $) and X-ray (2 keV) monochromatic luminosities and select only the model data points that agree with the observed UV-to-X-ray correlation. Our results show that the X-ray illumination of accretion disc model can reproduce the observed correlation for a subset of model configurations with a non-uniform distribution of black hole mass ($M_{\rm BH}$), accretion rate ($\dot{m}/\dot{m}_{\rm Edd}$), and power transferred from the accretion disc to the corona ($L_{\rm transf}/L_{\rm disc}$). In addition, our results reveal the presence of a correlation between $M_{\rm BH}$ and $\dot{m}/\dot{m}_{\rm Edd}$, and between $\dot{m}/\dot{m}_{\rm Edd}$ and $L_{\rm transf}/L_{\rm disc}$, to explain the observed X-ray-UV correlation. We also present evidence based on observed luminosities supporting our findings. We finally discuss the implications of our results.


**Translated Abstract**: 

已知在活跃星系核（AGN）中，紫外线（UV）和X射线发射之间有紧密的相关性。这一相关性在低红移和高红移源中均有观察到。特别是，对大规模类星体样本的观察揭示了UV和X射线之间非线性相关性的存在。该相关性的物理起源尚不清楚。在这项工作中，我们在中心源对吸积盘的X射线照射框架下探讨了这一观察到的相关性。我们在之前的工作中已展示该模型成功解释了AGN中连续的UV/光学时间延迟、变异性和宽带谱能分布。我们利用此模型生成了150,000个模型SED，假设模型参数均匀分布。计算相应的UV（2500Å）和X射线（2 keV）单色光度，并仅选择与观察到的UV到X射线相关性一致的模型数据点。结果表明，吸积盘的X射线照射模型能够重现观察到的相关性，前提是适合具有黑洞质量（M_{\rm BH}）、吸积率（\dot{m}/\dot{m}_{\rm Edd}）和从吸积盘传递到日冕的功率（L_{\rm transf}/L_{\rm disc}）的非均匀分布的模型配置。此外，结果揭示了M_{\rm BH}与\dot{m}/\dot{m}_{\rm Edd}之间，以及\dot{m}/\dot{m}_{\rm Edd}与L_{\rm transf}/L_{\rm disc}之间的相关性，以解释观察到的X射线-UV相关性。我们还根据观察到的光度提供了支持我们发现的证据。最后，我们讨论了结果的影响。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文研究了活跃星系核（AGN）中紫外线（UV）与X射线发射之间的紧密相关性，这一相关性在不同红移的源中均被广泛观察。

- (2): 过去的研究主要通过观察X射线和UV光度的变化关系来探讨这一相关性，但对其物理起源理解不足。与现有方法不同，本文提出了基于中心源对吸积盘进行X射线照射的模型，能够较好地解释UV与X射线之间的非线性相关性。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于展示了X射线照射模型可以重现UV到X射线的相关性，并识别出黑洞质量与吸积率之间的关系，从而加深了对AGN物理机制的理解。

- (4): 本研究的方法包括生成150,000个模型SED，并计算对应的UV（2500Å）和X射线（2 keV）单色光度，选择符合UV到X射线相关性的模型数据点进行分析。

- (5): 本文的方法在重现UV到X射线的相关性任务上取得了成功，表明研究目标得到了有效支持，为进一步理解AGN的能量生成机制提供了基础。


## MEGA Mass Assembly with JWST: The MIRI EGS Galaxy and AGN Survey
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.19078v2
- **Authors**: ['Bren E. Backhaus', 'Allison Kirkpatrick', 'Guang Yang', 'Gregory Troiani', 'Kurt Hamblin', 'Jeyhan S. Kartaltepe', 'Dale D. Kocevski', 'Anton M. Koekemoer', 'Erini Lambrides', 'Casey Papovich', 'Kaila Ronayne']
- **Abstrat**: We present the MIRI EGS Galaxy and AGN (MEGA) survey, a four band MIRI survey with 25 pointing in the Extended Groth Strip (EGS) extragalactic field. Three of the pointings utilized only the three reddest bands (F1000W, F1500W, F2100W) while the remainder of the pointings also add a blue filter (F770W). MEGA builds upon the existing observations in the EGS field by providing MIRI imaging for 68.9% of CEERS NIRCam imaging, filling a cruciality gap in order to understand galaxy evolution by observing the obscured Universe. Here, we present the technical design, data reduction, photometric catalog creation, the first data release, and science drivers of the MEGA survey. Our data reduction starts with the standard JWST calibration pipeline, but adds additional warm pixel masking and custom background subtraction steps to improve the quality of the final science image. We estimate the image depth of the reduced mosaics and present new galaxy number counts in four MIRI bands.


**Translated Abstract**: 

我们介绍了MIRI EGS Galaxy和AGN（MEGA）调查，这是一个在扩展的Groth带（EGS）外星场进行的四波段MIRI调查，共有25个指向。三项指向仅使用三个红色波段（F1000W、F1500W、F2100W），而其余指向还增加了一个蓝色滤光片（F770W）。MEGA在EGS领域现有观测的基础上，提供了68.9%的CEERS NIRCam成像，为理解星系演化填补了关键的空白。我们在这里展示了MEGA调查的技术设计、数据处理、光度目录创建、首个数据发布以及科学驱动。我们的数据处理从标准的JWST校准管道开始，增加了额外的温暖像素掩膜和定制背景减除步骤，以提高最终科学图像的质量。我们估计了减少马赛克的图像深度，并在四个MIRI波段中呈现新的星系数量计数。

**Summary**:

- (1): 文章的研究背景是中红外（MIR）观测能够透视尘埃，从而清晰地观察星系，并准确测量星系的特性，以研究星系的形成和演化。

- (2): 过去的方法主要使用如Spitzer和WISE等望远镜，这些方法存在低分辨率和无法观测到高红移星系的问题。本文提出的方法利用了JWST上的MIRI，此高分辨率可观察到z∼3的星系，解决了之前无法观察尘埃掩蔽区域的局限性，动机合理。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于首次提供了对68.9% CEERS NIRCam成像覆盖的MEGA调查数据，包含精细的数据处理和星系数量计数，助力理解星系和超大质量黑洞的共同演化。

- (4): 研究方法论包括在EGS区域内进行四波段的MIRI成像，使用多点指向和自定义的背景减除步骤，以创建高质量的光度目录和数量计数。

- (5): 本文的任务是进行星系数量计数，取得了新的结果，并且这些结果的性能支撑了他们对理解星系演化和黑洞活动的目标。


## Extended Emission Line Region in a Post-Starburst Galaxy Hosting TDE AT2019qiz and QPE
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.19722v2
- **Authors**: ['Yifei Xiong', 'Ning Jiang', 'Zhen Pan', 'Lei Hao', 'Zhenzhen Li']
- **Abstrat**: We present a comprehensive analysis of the extended emission line region (EELR) in the host galaxy of the tidal disruption event (TDE) AT2019qiz, utilizing VLT/MUSE integral-field spectroscopy. The high spatial-resolution data reveal a bi-conical emission structure approximately $3.7~\mathrm{kpc}$ in scale within the galactic center, characterized by a prominent [OIII] line in the nucleus and significant [NII] line emission extending into the EELR. Spectral analysis of the EELR indicates line ratios consistent with Seyfert ionization in the center and LINER-type ionization in the outer diffuse region, suggesting ionization from galactic nuclear activity. The required ionizing luminosity, estimated from the H$\rm{\alpha}$ and H$\rm{\beta}$ luminosities based on the photoionization and recombination balance assumption, is $10^{41.8}$ $\mathrm{erg\,s^{-1}}$ for all spaxels classified as AGN, and $10^{40.7}$ $\mathrm{erg\,s^{-1}}$ for spaxels in the central $0.9~\mathrm{kpc}$ Seyfert region. However, the current bolometric luminosity of the nucleus $L_{\text{bol}} \leq 10^{40.8}\,\mathrm{erg\,s^{-1}}$, estimated from quiescent-state soft X-ray observations, is insufficient to ionize the entire EELR, implying a recently faded AGN or a delayed response to historical activity. Stellar population analysis reveals a post-starburst characteristic in the EELR, and the gas kinematics show disturbances and non-circular components compared to the stellar kinematics. Notably, the recent detection of quasi-periodic eruptions (QPEs) in the X-ray light curve of AT2019qiz confirms the TDE-QPE association. Our findings provide direct evidence for an AGN-like EELR in the host galaxy of the nearest TDE with QPE detection, offering new insights into the complex interplay between TDEs, QPEs, AGN activity, and host galaxy evolution.


**Translated Abstract**: 本文对潮汐扰动事件（TDE）AT2019qiz宿主星系的扩展发射线区域（EELR）进行了全面分析，利用VLT/MUSE积分场光谱学。高空间分辨率数据揭示了一个大约3.7 kpc规模的双锥发射结构，在星系中心以显著的[O III]线为特征，并且有显著的[N II]线发射延伸到EELR中。对EELR的光谱分析表明，星中心的线比率与 Seyfert 类型电离一致，而外部弥散区域则表现为LINER类型电离，表明源自星系核的活动所致。根据光电离和复合平衡假设，从Hα和Hβ光度估计所需的电离光度，对于所有分类为AGN的像元估计为$10^{41.8}$ $\mathrm{erg\,s^{-1}}$，而对于位于中央0.9 kpc Seyfert区域的像元则为$10^{40.7}$ $\mathrm{erg\,s^{-1}}$。然而，估计的当前核的整体光度$L_{\text{bol}} \leq 10^{40.8}\,\mathrm{erg\,s^{-1}}$，不足以电离整个EELR，暗示一个近期衰退的AGN或历史活动的延迟响应。恒星种群分析揭示了EELR中的后暴发特征，气体运动学显示出了相较于恒星运动学的扰动和非圆形成分。值得注意的是，AT2019qiz的X射线光曲线中最近检测到的准周期性爆发（QPE）确认了TDE-QPE关联。我们的研究结果为最近的TDE与QPE检测中的宿主星系提供了直接的AGN-like EELR证据，并为TDE、QPE、AGN活动及宿主星系演化之间的复杂相互作用提供了新的见解。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文研究背景为潮汐扰动事件（TDE）和准周期性爆发（QPE）在星系核中近年的观测趋势，着重探索二者间的联系及其对宿主星系演化的影响。

- (2): 过去的方法主要是对TDE和QPE的单独观察和分析，存在的主要问题是对其相互关系及宿主星系特征的缺乏综合研究。本文通过利用VLT/MUSE光谱获取高分辨率数据，提出数据综合分析的方法，显著提升了对EELR电离机制及星系活动状态的理解，因此具有合理动机。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于揭示了AT2019qiz宿主星系中的AGN-like EELR特征，并通过具体数据支持了TDE与QPE之间可能的物理联系，为后续研究提供了重要资料和新视角。

- (4): 本文研究的方法论包括对VLT/MUSE光谱数据的深度分析，结合光谱比率及光度估算，系统探讨了EELR中的电离特征及其与AGNs的关系。

- (5): 本文在识别TDE宿主星系的EELR特征以及电离机制的深入研究中取得了突破性成果，显著地支持了TDE与QPE的联系，这与研究目标一致，提升了对星系核活动及其演化的理解。


## Massive black hole formation in Population III star clusters
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.20415v1
- **Authors**: ['B. Reinoso', 'M. A. Latif', 'D. R. G. Schleicher']
- **Abstrat**: The James Webb Space Telescope (JWST) has revealed a population of active galactic nuclei (AGNs) that challenge existing black hole (BH) formation models. These newly observed BHs are overmassive compared to the host galaxies and have an unexpectedly high abundance. Their exact origin remains elusive. The primary goal of this work is to investigate the formation of massive BH seeds in dense Population III (Pop III) star clusters. Using a cosmological simulation of Pop III cluster formation, we present models for the assembly and subsequent evolution of these clusters. The models account for background gas potential, stellar collisions and associated mass loss, gas accretion, stellar growth, their initial mass function (IMF), and subsequent star formation. We conduct $N$-body simulations of these models over a span of 2 million years. Our results show that BHs of $> 400$ M$_\odot$ are formed in all cases, reaching up to $\sim 5000$ M$_\odot$ under optimistic yet reasonable conditions and potentially exceeding 10$^4$ M$_\odot$ provided that high accretion rates of 10$^{-3}$ M$_\odot$ yr$^{-1}$ onto the stars can be sustained. We conclude that massive BHs can be formed in Pop III stellar clusters and are likely to remain within their host clusters. These BHs may experience further growth as they sink into the galaxy's potential well. This formation channel should be given further consideration in models of galaxy formation and BH demographics.


**Translated Abstract**: 

詹姆斯·韦布空间望远镜（JWST）揭示了一些活跃星系核（AGN），这些AGN在质量上与宿主星系不成比例，而且数量超出预期。它们的确切起源仍然模糊不清。本文的主要目标是研究在密集的第三类星群(population III, Pop III)中形成大量黑洞种子的过程。我们使用第三类星群形成的宇宙学模拟，展示了这些星群的组装及其后续演化模型。这些模型考虑了背景气体势、恒星碰撞及相应的质量损失、气体吸积、恒星生长、以及它们的初始质量函数（IMF）及其后续的恒星形成。我们进行了长达200万年的N体模拟。结果显示，所有情况下都形成了质量超过400 M⊙的黑洞，在乐观的条件下，质量可达约5000 M⊙，并且在高达10^{-3} M⊙ yr^{-1}的吸积率下，可能超过10^4 M⊙。我们得出结论，巨型黑洞可以在第三类恒星团中形成，并可能留在其宿主星团内。这些黑洞在下沉到星系的引力井中时可能会经历进一步的生长。这种形成通道应该在星系形成和黑洞人口学模型中获得更大关注。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文的研究背景是JWST观测到的活跃星系核（AGN）数量超出现有黑洞形成模型的预期，这表明超大质量黑洞的形成机制仍然不明。

- (2): 过去的方法主要依赖于对第一代恒星（Pop III）的质量函数进行静态模型模拟，但存在恒星形成后质量耗损及气体迅速耗尽等问题。提出的方法通过结合宇宙学模拟与更多物理过程（如气体吸积和恒星碰撞）来填补这些空白。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于展示了在密集的Pop III恒星星团中形成超过400 M⊙的巨型黑洞的可能性，并提出这一过程可能对星系形成和黑洞的形成与演化有重要影响。

- (4): 本文采用宇宙学模拟方法，结合N体模拟，研究了Pop III星团的组装与演化过程，并分析了其对黑洞形成的影响。

- (5): 本文的方法在研究中成功预测了形成超过400 M⊙的黑洞，并指出在高吸积率条件下可达到规模更大的黑洞，这表明其方法的有效性支持了研究目标。


## Witnessing the onset of reionisation via Lyman-$α$ emission at redshift 13
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2408.16608v4
- **Authors**: ['Joris Witstok', 'Peter Jakobsen', 'Roberto Maiolino', 'Jakob M. Helton', 'Benjamin D. Johnson', 'Brant E. Robertson', 'Sandro Tacchella', 'Alex J. Cameron', 'Renske Smit', 'Andrew J. Bunker', 'Aayush Saxena', 'Fengwu Sun', 'Stacey Alberts', 'Santiago Arribas', 'William M. Baker', 'Rachana Bhatawdekar', 'Kristan Boyett', 'Phillip A. Cargile', 'Stefano Carniani', 'Stéphane Charlot', 'Jacopo Chevallard', 'Mirko Curti', 'Emma Curtis-Lake', "Francesco D'Eugenio", 'Daniel J. Eisenstein', 'Kevin N. Hainline', 'Gareth C. Jones', 'Nimisha Kumari', 'Michael V. Maseda', 'Pablo G. Pérez-González', 'Pierluigi Rinaldi', 'Jan Scholtz', 'Hannah Übler', 'Christina C. Williams', 'Christopher N. A. Willmer', 'Chris Willott', 'Yongda Zhu']
- **Abstrat**: $\require{mediawiki-texvc}$Cosmic Reionisation commenced when ultraviolet (UV) radiation produced in the first galaxies began illuminating the cold, neutral gas that filled the primordial Universe. Recent James Webb Space Telescope (JWST) observations have shown that surprisingly UV-bright galaxies were in place beyond redshift $z = 14$, when the Universe was less than $300 \, \mathrm{Myr}$ old. Smooth turnovers of their UV continua have been interpreted as damping-wing absorption of Lyman-$\alpha$ (Ly$\alpha$), the principal hydrogen transition. However, spectral signatures encoding crucial properties of these sources, such as their emergent radiation field, largely remain elusive. Here we report spectroscopy from the JWST Advanced Deep Extragalactic Survey (JADES) of a galaxy at redshift $z = 13.0$ that reveal a singular, bright emission line unambiguously identified as Ly$\alpha$, in addition to a smooth turnover. We observe an equivalent width of $\text{EW}_\mathrm{Ly\alpha} > 40 \, \AA$ (rest frame), previously only seen at $z < 9$ where the intervening intergalactic medium (IGM) becomes increasingly ionised. Together with an extremely blue UV continuum, the unexpected Ly$\alpha$ emission indicates the galaxy is a prolific producer and leaker of ionising photons. This suggests massive, hot stars or an active galactic nucleus (AGN) have created an early reionised region to prevent complete extinction of Ly$\alpha$, thus shedding new light on the nature of the earliest galaxies and the onset of Reionisation only $330 \, \mathrm{Myr}$ after the Big Bang.


**Translated Abstract**: 

宇宙重离子化的开始是由第一批星系产生的紫外（UV）辐射照亮充满初始宇宙的冷中性气体所引发的。最近的詹姆斯·韦布太空望远镜（JWST）观测显示在红移 z = 14 之上意外地存在亮度很高的星系，这个时候宇宙不到 300 百万年。它们的UV光谱曲线平滑的转折被解读为莱曼α（Lyα）的阻尼翼吸收。然而，这些源的光谱特征，尤其是其辐射场的信息，仍然相当模糊。在这篇文章中，我们报告了 JWST 深层外星系调查（JADES）对一个红移 z = 13.0 的星系进行的光谱观测，我们发现了一条单一且明亮的发射线，明确识别为 Lyα，此外还有平滑的转折。我们观察到 Lyα 的等效宽度 EW_Lyα > 40 Å（在休息帧），这在 z < 9 之间才有观察记录，而当时介于星际介质（IGM）的中性度逐渐增高。结合极蓝的 UV 光谱曲线，意外的 Lyα 发射表明该星系是一个强大的电离光子生产者和漏出者。这表明大质量、热的恒星或活跃星系核（AGN）创建了一个早期重离子化区域，从而阻止了 Lyα 的完全消失，这为最早的星系及重离子化的开始提供了新的视角，仅在大爆炸后 330 百万年时发生。

**Summary**:

- (1): 该文章的研究背景是宇宙重离子化的首次发生，研究表明第一批星系产生的紫外辐射开始影响初始宇宙中的中性气体。

- (2): 过去的方法主要基于观测星系的UV光谱曲线与Lyα的阻尼翼吸收，然而对于来源的辐射场特征缺乏直接的证据。本文提出的方法通过JWST光谱观测能够直接探测到Lyα发射线，克服了以往方法注重吸收而忽视发射的缺陷，且有充分的动机支持这一研究。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于首次在红移z = 13的星系中确认Lyα明亮发射线的存在，提供了对早期星系和宇宙重离子化过程的新见解。

- (4): 本文的研究方法是利用JWST的NIRSpec进行深度光谱观测，通过高信噪比探测到Lyα发射线，以及对UV光谱连续光谱特征的分析。

- (5): 文章在红移z = 13.0的星系上实现了对Lyα发射的直接观测，提供了EW_Lyα > 40 Å的结果，这一性能对支持研究的目标是充分的。


## A multi-scale investigation into the diagnostic potential of the HCN/HCO$^+$ ratio for AGN and starburst activity in nearby galaxies
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.19527v2
- **Authors**: ['J. Butterworth', 'S. Viti', 'Y. Wang']
- **Abstrat**: (Abridged) The identification of AGN and SB regions in galaxies is crucial for understanding the role of various physical processes in galaxy evolution. Molecular line ratios, such as the HCN/HCO+ ratio, have been proposed as potential tracers of these distinct environments. This paper aims to assess the reliability of the HCN/HCO+ ratio, from J = 1-0 to J = 4-3 transitions, as a diagnostic tool for differentiating AGN and SB activity across a diverse sample of nearby galaxies. We focus on evaluating the effect of spatial resolution on the robustness of these ratios and investigate the underlying physical conditions that drive observed variations. We compile observations of HCN and HCO+ lines across multiple J transitions from various sources, covering different galaxy types, including Seyferts, starbursts, and (ultra-)luminous infrared galaxies (U/LIRGs). The observations span spatial scales from cloud-sized regions to kiloparsec scales. We analyse the behaviour of these ratios at varying resolutions and employ non-LTE radiative transfer models to infer the physical conditions that drive the observed ratios. We find that the HCN/HCO+ ratio from higher J transitions can differentiate between AGN and SB activity when observed at high spatial resolution. This distinction occurs around unity. However, at lower resolutions, contamination from multiple emission sources and beam averaging effects destroy these distinctions. Modelling suggests that elevated HCN/HCO+ ratios in AGN-dominated regions are largely driven by an enhancement in HCN abundance relative to HCO+, likely due to high-temperature chemistry or increased excitation. Our study confirms that the HCN/HCO+ ratio, particularly of higher J transitions, can be a reliable tracer of AGN versus SB activity if observations are conducted at sufficiently high spatial resolution.


**Translated Abstract**: 

（缩略）活跃星系核（AGN）与星暴（SB）区域的识别对于理解星系演化中的各种物理过程至关重要。分子线比率，如 HCN/HCO+比率，被提出作为这些不同环境的潜在探测器。本文旨在评估 HCN/HCO+比率（从 J = 1-0 到 J = 4-3跃迁）作为区分AGN和SB活性的诊断工具的可靠性。我们重点评估空间分辨率对这些比率稳健性的影响，并研究驱动观察到的变化的基本物理条件。我们编译了来自不同来源的多个 J跃迁的 HCN 和 HCO+线观测，覆盖包括 Seyferts、星暴及（超）亮红外星系（U/LIRGs）在内的不同星系类型，观测的空间尺度从云状区域到千秒差距尺度。我们分析了这些比率在不同分辨率下的行为，并采用非 LTE 辐射传输模型推断驱动观察到的比率的物理条件。我们发现，在高空间分辨率下观察的高 J跃迁的 HCN/HCO+比率可以区分AGN和SB活性。这一区分发生在接近1的地方。然而，在较低分辨率下，多个发射源的污染和光束平均效应破坏了这些区分。建模表明，AGN主导区域中HCN/HCO+比率的升高主要是由于 HCN 相对于 HCO+的丰度增加，这可能是由于高温化学或更高的激发所致。我们的研究确认，高 J跃迁的 HCN/HCO+比率在足够高的空间分辨率观测条件下，能够可靠地作为AGN与SB活性的探测器。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文的研究背景是探讨活跃星系核（AGN）与星暴（SB）区域在星系演化中的重要性及其物理过程。

- (2): 过去的方法主要使用分子线比率如 HCN/HCO+来区分AGN和SB活性，存在较低分辨率导致污染与光束平均效应的问题。本文提出的高空间分辨率观察方法克服了这些问题，验证了高 J跃迁的 HCN/HCO+比率作为诊断工具的可靠性，具有较强的驱动理由。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于确认了高 J跃迁的 HCN/HCO+比率在高空间分辨率条件下，能够有效地区分AGN与SB活性，并揭示了其背后的物理机制。

- (4): 本文采用的研究方法包括编制多种星系类型的 HCN和 HCO+观测数据，分析不同分辨率下的比率表现，并利用非 LTE 辐射传输模型推导物理条件。

- (5): 本文方法在高空间分辨率下对 HCN/HCO+比率进行分析，成功区分出AGN与SB区域的活动，这一表现支持了其作为诊断工具的目标。


## A consistent radio to sub-mm pc-scale study of the nucleus of NGC 1068
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.20303v1
- **Authors**: ['Isaac M. Mutie', 'Santiago del Palacio', 'Robert J. Beswick', 'David Williams-Baldwin', 'Jack F. Gallimore', 'John S. Gallagher', 'Susanne E. Aalto', 'Paul O. Baki']
- **Abstrat**: The origin of radio emission in radio-quiet (RQ) AGN remains a long-standing mystery. We present a detailed study of the cm to sub-mm emission from the nucleus of the nearby prototypical RQ Seyfert 2 galaxy, NGC 1068. We analyse observations between 4.5-706 GHz using $e$-MERLIN, VLA and ALMA. We restricted all data used for imaging to a matching $uv-$range of 15$-$3300 k$\lambda$, to ensure that all data sampled the same spatial scales. All images were restored with a $\sim$ 0.06$''$ beam. To derive the spectral energy distribution (SED), we fit synchrotron, free-free, dust and coronal component models to these data. We report that the sub-mm excess between $\sim$ 200-700 GHz is consistent with synchrotron emission from a compact and optically thick corona with a radius $R_\mathrm{c}\approx 70\pm5 \,R_\mathrm{g}$, a fraction of $\sim$\,$10\pm2$% of the energy density in the form of non-thermal electrons, and a magnetic field strength $B\approx 148$ G. The luminosity of the corona is roughly consistent with -- though higher than -- the expected from mm--X-ray correlations derived in recent studies of RQ AGN. This difference is likely due to the corona SED peaking at ($\approx$550 GHz). Between 10 and $\sim$ 200 GHz, the SED is dominated by free-free emission. High angular resolution observations at frequencies below 5 GHz are needed to constrain a putative optically thin synchrotron component and the amount of free-free absorption.


**Translated Abstract**: 

在无线电安静（RQ）活动星系核（AGN）中，无线电辐射的来源仍然是一个长期未解的谜团。我们对附近的原型 RQ Seyfert 2 银河NGC 1068 核心的厘米到亚毫米（sub-mm）辐射进行了详细研究。我们分析了 4.5-706 GHz 的观测数据，使用了$e$-MERLIN、VLA 和 ALMA。我们将所有用于成像的数据限制在 15-3300 k$\lambda$ 的相同 $uv$ 范围内，以确保所有数据采样相同的空间尺度。所有图像均使用约0.06$''$的波束恢复。为了得出光谱能量分布（SED），我们对这些数据拟合了同步辐射、自由-自由、尘埃和日冕成分模型。我们报告称，在200-700 GHz之间的亚毫米过量与来自一个半径约为$R_\mathrm{c} \approx 70 \pm 5 \,R_\mathrm{g}$且光学厚的日冕的同步辐射发射一致，其中约有 10±2% 的能量密度以非热电子的形式存在，磁场强度$B \approx 148$ G。日冕的光度与近期 RQ AGN 研究中推导的毫米—X 射线相关性大致一致，但略高。这一差异可能是因为日冕 SED 的峰值位于（约 550 GHz）。在 10 和 200 GHz 之间，SED 主要由自由-自由辐射主导。需要在 5 GHz 以下进行高角分辨率观测，以限制一个假定的光学薄同步辐射成分和自由-自由吸收的量。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文研究背景为无无线电辐射的活动星系核（RQ AGN）中无线电发射的起源仍然未明，特别是针对NGC 1068这一近邻RQ Seyfert 2银河。

- (2): 之前的方法是使用不同的干涉观测数据构建光谱能量分布（SED），但存在空间尺度采样不一致及冲突的光谱结果等问题。本文的方法通过将所有数据限制在相同的$uv$范围内，解决了这一问题，确保了对相同空间尺度一致性的分析。

- (3): 论文的贡献在于明确了NGC 1068的亚毫米辐射过量是同步辐射的结果，并提出了一个光学厚的日冕模型，从而深化了我们对RQ AGN无线电发射机制的理解。

- (4): 本文采用的方法包括综合分析4.5-706 GHz的各种观测数据，拟合同步辐射、自由-自由筏发射和尘埃成分模型，以准确描述SED。

- (5): 该方法实现了对NGC 1068无线电到亚毫米波长辐射的详细分析，揭示了日冕辐射特性，为进一步研究RQ AGN提供了坚实的基础，证明了其研究目标的可行性。


# ALMA
## A consistent radio to sub-mm pc-scale study of the nucleus of NGC 1068
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.20303v1
- **Authors**: ['Isaac M. Mutie', 'Santiago del Palacio', 'Robert J. Beswick', 'David Williams-Baldwin', 'Jack F. Gallimore', 'John S. Gallagher', 'Susanne E. Aalto', 'Paul O. Baki']
- **Abstrat**: The origin of radio emission in radio-quiet (RQ) AGN remains a long-standing mystery. We present a detailed study of the cm to sub-mm emission from the nucleus of the nearby prototypical RQ Seyfert 2 galaxy, NGC 1068. We analyse observations between 4.5-706 GHz using $e$-MERLIN, VLA and ALMA. We restricted all data used for imaging to a matching $uv-$range of 15$-$3300 k$\lambda$, to ensure that all data sampled the same spatial scales. All images were restored with a $\sim$ 0.06$''$ beam. To derive the spectral energy distribution (SED), we fit synchrotron, free-free, dust and coronal component models to these data. We report that the sub-mm excess between $\sim$ 200-700 GHz is consistent with synchrotron emission from a compact and optically thick corona with a radius $R_\mathrm{c}\approx 70\pm5 \,R_\mathrm{g}$, a fraction of $\sim$\,$10\pm2$% of the energy density in the form of non-thermal electrons, and a magnetic field strength $B\approx 148$ G. The luminosity of the corona is roughly consistent with -- though higher than -- the expected from mm--X-ray correlations derived in recent studies of RQ AGN. This difference is likely due to the corona SED peaking at ($\approx$550 GHz). Between 10 and $\sim$ 200 GHz, the SED is dominated by free-free emission. High angular resolution observations at frequencies below 5 GHz are needed to constrain a putative optically thin synchrotron component and the amount of free-free absorption.


**Translated Abstract**: 

在无线电安静（RQ）活跃星系核（AGN）中，无线电辐射的来源仍然是一个长期存在的谜题。我们对附近原型RQ Seyfert 2星系NGC 1068的核区域进行了详细的厘米到亚毫米波段的研究。我们分析了使用 $e$-MERLIN、VLA和ALMA在4.5-706 GHz范围内的观测数据。为了确保所有数据采样相同的空间尺度，我们将用于成像的所有数据限制在匹配的 $uv-$范围15-3300 k$\lambda$内。所有图像以约0.06$''$的光束恢复。为了推导光谱能量分布（SED），我们对这些数据进行同步加速、自由-自由、尘埃和日冕成分模型的拟合。我们报告说，约200-700 GHz之间的亚毫米过剩与来自半径为 $R_\mathrm{c}\approx 70\pm5 \,R_\mathrm{g}$ 的紧凑且光学厚的日冕的同步加速辐射一致，其中约有10±2%的能量密度以非热电子的形式存在，磁场强度为 $B\approx 148$ G。日冕的光度大致与最近关于RQ AGN的mm–X射线相关研究的预期一致，尽管偏高。这一差异可能是由于日冕 SED 在 ($\approx$ 550 GHz) 附近达到了峰值。在10到约200 GHz之间，SED主要由自由-自由辐射主导。在5 GHz以下的高角分辨率观测对于限制可能存在的光学薄同步辐射成分和自由-自由吸收量是必要的。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文的研究背景是无线电安静（RQ）活跃星系核（AGN）中无线电辐射来源的长期谜题，特别是聚焦于原型RQ Seyfert 2星系NGC 1068。

- (2): 过去的方法主要通过不同的干涉观测处理无线电-亚毫米波段的数据，存在对比数据集时由于采样范围和角度分辨率不同而导致结果矛盾的问题。本文提出的方法通过限制数据在相同的 $uv-$ 范围来解决这一点，确保所有数据采样相同的空间尺度，从而提供了一个更一致和可靠的光谱能量分布（SED）。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于揭示NGC 1068核区亚毫米波段的辐射机制，表明在200-700 GHz范围内的过剩与日冕的同步加速辐射一致，这为研究RQ AGN中的无线电辐射起源提供了新的洞见。

- (4): 本文的研究方法包括通过使用 $e$-MERLIN、VLA 和 ALMA 对数据进行处理和成像，同时使用同步加速、自由-自由、尘埃和日冕成分模型来拟合所获得的数据，从而得出SED。

- (5): 本文的方法任务是构建和分析NGC 1068的无线电到亚毫米波段的SED，报告表明日冕辐射的光度与预期相符。尽管有些偏高的结果，文中对SED的分析和日冕的建模展现了一个可行的方向，支持作者对于理解RQ AGN辐射机制的目标。

## Utilizing Stellar Mass Estimates to Identify Gravitational Wave Host Galaxies
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.20777v1
- **Authors**: ['M. Pálfi', 'G. Dálya', 'P. Raffai']
- **Abstrat**: Stellar mass can enhance the ranking of potential hosts for compact binary coalescences identified by ground-based gravitational-wave detectors within large localisation areas containing even thousands of galaxies. Despite its benefits, accurate stellar mass estimation is often time-consuming and computationally intensive. In this study, we implement four stellar mass estimation methods based on infrared magnitudes and compare them with values estimated with spectral energy distribution fitting from GAMA DR3, revealing strong correlations. We also introduce a method to calibrate the results from these estimation methods to match the reference values. Our analysis of simulated binary black hole events demonstrates that incorporating stellar mass improves the rank of actual hosts ~80 per cent of cases. Furthermore, the improvement is comparable when stellar masses are derived from the tested estimation methods to when they are obtained directly from the simulated galaxy catalogue, demonstrating that simple stellar mass estimates can provide a computationally efficient alternative.


**Translated Abstract**: 

恒星质量可以提高已经通过地面引力波探测器识别的紧凑双星并合事件的潜在宿主的排名，即使在包含数千个星系的大定位区域内。尽管有其好处，但准确的恒星质量估计往往耗时且计算密集。本研究基于红外光度实施了四种恒星质量估计方法，并与来自 GAMA DR3 的光谱能量分布拟合估计值进行了比较，揭示了强相关性。我们还引入了一种校准这些估计方法结果以匹配参考值的方法。对模拟的双黑洞事件的分析表明，纳入恒星质量改善了约 80% 实际宿主的排名。此外，当恒星质量来自于测试的估计方法时，改善与从模拟星系目录直接获得的恒星质量相当，这表明简单的恒星质量估计可以提供计算上高效的替代方案。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文的研究背景是如何利用引力波探测器识别紧凑双星并合事件的宿主星系。

- (2): 过去的方法主要应用了几种基于光谱能量分布或红外光度的恒星质量估计，但这些方法通常耗时且计算复杂。本研究提出的方法通过简化恒星质量估计过程，使用红外光度估计恒星质量，解决了计算效率低的问题，这一方法得到了良好的理论支持。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于实现了四种恒星质量估计方法的比较，并引入了一种校准方法，证明了这一方法可以有效提升识别双黑洞事件宿主的准确性。

- (5): 本文的方法在识别双黑洞事件的宿主星系任务中，约 80% 的情况下提升了宿主的排名，表明该方法在实现其目标方面具有有效性。


## Validation of the DESI DR2 Measurements of Baryon Acoustic Oscillations from Galaxies and Quasars
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.14742v2
- **Authors**: ['U. Andrade', 'E. Paillas', 'J. Mena-Fernández', 'Q. Li', 'A. J. Ross', 'S. Nadathur', 'M. Rashkovetskyi', 'A. Pérez-Fernández', 'H. Seo', 'N. Sanders', 'O. Alves', 'X. Chen', 'N. Huterer', 'M. Ishak', 'S. Juneau', 'R. Kehoe', 'D. Kirkby', 'T. Kisner', 'A. Kremin', 'O. Lahav', 'C. Lamman', 'M. Landriau', 'L. Le Guillou', 'A. Leauthaud', 'M. E. Levi', 'C. Magneville', 'M. Manera', 'P. Martini', 'W. Matthewson', 'A. Meisner', 'R. Miquel', 'J. Moustakas', 'A. Muñoz-Gutiérrez', 'D. Muñoz-Santos', 'A. D. Myers', 'L. Napolitano', 'J. A. Newman', 'H. E. Noriega', 'N. Palanque-Delabrouille', 'J. Pan', 'W. J. Percival', 'I. Pérez-Ràfols', 'C. Poppett', 'F. Prada', 'A. Raichoor', 'C. Ramírez-Pérez', 'C. Ravoux', 'G. Rossi', 'R. Ruggeri', 'L. Samushia', 'E. Sanchez', 'D. Schlegel', 'M. Schubnell', 'F. Sinigaglia', 'D. Sprayberry', 'T. Tan', 'G. Tarlé', 'P. Taylor', 'W. Turner', 'R. Vaisakh', 'M. Vargas-Magaña', 'M. Walther', 'B. A. Weaver', 'M. - **Abstrat**: The Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument (DESI) data release 2 (DR2) galaxy and quasar clustering data represents a significant expansion of data from DR1, providing improved statistical precision in BAO constraints across multiple tracers, including bright galaxies (BGS), luminous red galaxies (LRGs), emission line galaxies (ELGs), and quasars (QSOs). In this paper, we validate the BAO analysis of DR2. We present the results of robustness tests on the blinded DR2 data and, after unblinding, consistency checks on the unblinded DR2 data. All results are compared to those obtained from a suite of mock catalogs that replicate the selection and clustering properties of the DR2 sample. We confirm the consistency of DR2 BAO measurements with DR1 while achieving a reduction in statistical uncertainties due to the increased survey volume and completeness. We assess the impact of analysis choices, including different data vectors (correlation function vs. power spectrum), modeling approaches and systematics treatments, and an assumption of the Gaussian likelihood, finding that our BAO constraints are stable across these variations and assumptions with a few minor refinements to the baseline setup of the DR1 BAO analysis. We summarize a series of pre-unblinding tests that confirmed the readiness of our analysis pipeline, the final systematic errors, and the DR2 BAO analysis baseline. The successful completion of these tests led to the unblinding of the DR2 BAO measurements, ultimately leading to the DESI DR2 cosmological analysis, with their implications for the expansion history of the Universe and the nature of dark energy presented in the DESI key paper.


**Translated Abstract**: 

暗能量光谱仪（DESI）第二次数据发布（DR2）中的星系和类星体聚类数据显著扩展了来自DR1的数据，通过多种迹象（包括明亮星系（BGS）、发光红星系（LRGs）、发射线星系（ELGs）和类星体（QSOs））提供了更高统计精度的BAO约束。在本文中，我们验证了DR2的BAO分析。我们展示了对盲测DR2数据的稳健性测试的结果，并在解盲后，对解盲的DR2数据进行了一致性检查。所有结果都与一系列模拟目录进行了比较，这些模拟目录复制了DR2样本的选择和聚类特性。我们确认DR2 BAO测量结果与DR1一致，同时由于新增的调查体积和完整性，统计不确定性得以减少。我们评估了分析选择的影响，包括不同数据向量（相关函数与功率谱）、建模方法和系统处理以及高斯似然假设的影响，发现我们的BAO约束在这些变化和假设中保持稳定，但对DR1 BAO分析的基线设置作了一些小的改进。我们总结了一系列解盲前的测试，证明了我们分析管道的准备状态、最终系统误差以及DR2 BAO分析的基线。成功完成这些测试后，我们解盲了DR2 BAO测量结果，最终导致了DESI DR2的宇宙学分析，并在DESI关键论文中展示了其对宇宙扩展历史和暗能量性质的影响。

**Summary**:

- (3): 本文的贡献在于提供了DR2 BAO测量的验证，以及在解盲前后的系统性测试，确保数据分析的可靠性，并与DR1结果的一致性。

## Imprints of Stellar Feedback on Magnetic Fields in the Iris Nebula NGC 7023
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.20721v1
- **Authors**: ['Ekta Sharma', 'Kate Pattle', 'Di Li', 'Chang Won Lee', 'Maheswar Gopinathan', 'Tao-Chung Ching', 'Mehrnoosh Tahani', 'Shinyoung Kim']
- **Abstrat**: We present 850 $\mu$m polarized continuum observations carried out with the POL-2 polarimeter mounted on the James Clerk Maxwell Telescope (JCMT) towards NGC 7023 located in the Cepheus Flare region. NGC 7023 is a reflection nebula powered by a Herbig Ae Be star HD 200775 and also identified as a hub in the hub-filament cloud, LDN 1172/1174. We detect submillimetre emission well towards the northern (identified as C1) and the eastern region of the reflection nebula. We investigated the polarization structure and the magnetic field (B-field) morphology, which is found to be curved and follows the clump morphology. The comparison of the B-field morphology at the clump scales ($\sim$0.02 pc) with that of the envelope ($\sim$0.5 pc) suggests that the field lines are not preserved from envelope to clump scales, implying that an external factor may be responsible for disturbing the B-field structure. We estimated a magnetic field strength of 179$\pm$50 $\mu$G in the starless core, 121$\pm$34 $\mu$G in the protostellar core with a class I source and 150$\pm$42 $\mu$G in the protostellar core with a class II source using the $N_{2}H^{+}$ (1-0) line observed with 13.7 m single dish radio telescope at Taeduk Radio Astronomy Observatory (TRAO). The stability analysis using these B-field strengths gives magnetically sub-critical values, while the magnetic, gravitational, and outflow kinetic energies are roughly balanced. We also suggest that the reordering of the magnetic field lines could be due to the interaction with the already evolved high-velocity outflow gas around the central star, which hints at the presence of outflow feedback.


**Translated Abstract**: 

我们展示了在Cepheus Flare区域的NGC 7023进行的850 μm偏振连续观测，使用了安装在James Clerk Maxwell Telescope (JCMT)上的POL-2偏振仪。NGC 7023是一个由Herbig Ae Be star HD 200775提供能量的反射星云，且被识别为hub-filament云LDN 1172/1174中的一个中心。我们在反射星云的北部（标识为C1）和东部地区检测到亚毫米辐射。我们研究了偏振结构和磁场（B-field）形态，发现磁场呈弯曲形状并符合团块形态。在团块尺度（约0.02 pc）与包围尺度（约0.5 pc）上对比的B-field形态表明，磁场线在这两个尺度间并未保持一致，暗示可能存在外部因素干扰B-field结构。我们估计了星无星核中磁场强度为179±50 μG，在具有I类源的原恒星核中为121±34 μG，在具有II类源的原恒星核中为150±42 μG，数据来自在Taeduk Radio Astronomy Observatory (TRAO)上使用13.7 m单 dish射电望远镜观察的N2H+ (1-0)线。通过这些B-field强度进行稳定性分析得到的值为磁学亚临界，磁能、引力能和出流动能量大致平衡。我们还建议磁场线的重新排序可能是由于与中心恒星周围已经演化的高速度出流气体的相互作用，这暗示了出流反馈的存在。

**Summary**:


- (1): 本文的研究背景是磁场在天体物理过程中，尤其是在星际介质和星形成过程中扮演的重要角色，NGC 7023作为被星星照亮的反射星云是研究这一过程的理想对象。

- (2): 过去的方法主要依赖于不同波长的光学测量和三维辐射磁流体动力学模拟，存在对中等质量恒星附近磁场力量和形态的研究不足的问题。本文采用850 μm的偏振连续观测，具备高灵敏度和直接测量的优势，从而解决了以往对中质量恒星磁场研究的局限性，具有良好的动机。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于揭示了NGC 7023反射星云中磁场的形态及其与恒星反馈的关系，提供了更为明确的磁场强度数据，促进了对中等质量恒星附近气体动态和磁场作用的理解。

- (4): 本文的研究方法为使用POL-2偏振仪在JCMT进行850 μm偏振连续观测，并结合使用13.7 m单 dish射电望远镜观察N2H+ (1-0)线来估计磁场强度和形态。

- (5): 方法在反射星云NGC 7023中成功获取了磁场强度数据，以及探讨了磁场与星际气体的相互作用，表现出磁场和引力团队能量的近似平衡，这能够支持对中等质量恒星和其周围磁场动态的研究目标。


## MEGA Mass Assembly with JWST: The MIRI EGS Galaxy and AGN Survey
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.19078v2
- **Authors**: ['Bren E. Backhaus', 'Allison Kirkpatrick', 'Guang Yang', 'Gregory Troiani', 'Kurt Hamblin', 'Jeyhan S. Kartaltepe', 'Dale D. Kocevski', 'Anton M. Koekemoer', 'Erini Lambrides', 'Casey Papovich', 'Kaila Ronayne']
- **Abstrat**: We present the MIRI EGS Galaxy and AGN (MEGA) survey, a four band MIRI survey with 25 pointing in the Extended Groth Strip (EGS) extragalactic field. Three of the pointings utilized only the three reddest bands (F1000W, F1500W, F2100W) while the remainder of the pointings also add a blue filter (F770W). MEGA builds upon the existing observations in the EGS field by providing MIRI imaging for 68.9% of CEERS NIRCam imaging, filling a cruciality gap in order to understand galaxy evolution by observing the obscured Universe. Here, we present the technical design, data reduction, photometric catalog creation, the first data release, and science drivers of the MEGA survey. Our data reduction starts with the standard JWST calibration pipeline, but adds additional warm pixel masking and custom background subtraction steps to improve the quality of the final science image. We estimate the image depth of the reduced mosaics and present new galaxy number counts in four MIRI bands.


**Translated Abstract**: 

我们呈现了MIRI EGS银河和活动星系核（MEGA）调查，这是一个四波段的MIRI调查，在扩展的Groth带（EGS）外星场进行25个观测点的观测。三个观测点仅利用了三个红波段（F1000W，F1500W，F2100W），而其余的观测点则额外使用了一个蓝色滤波器（F770W）。MEGA建立在EGS领域现有观测的基础上，提供68.9% CEERS NIRCam成像的MIRI成像，填补了理解通过观察被遮蔽的宇宙来研究星系演化的关键空白。本文介绍了MEGA调查的技术设计、数据减缩、光度目录创建、首次数据发布和科学目标。我们的数据减缩从标准的JWST校准管道开始，但添加了额外的热像素掩蔽和自定义背景减法步骤，以提高最终科学图像的质量。我们估计了减缩马赛克的图像深度，并在四个MIRI波段中提供了新的星系数量计数。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文的研究背景是通过中红外（MIR）观察研究星系的形成与演化，尤其是在宇宙遮蔽区的星系。

- (2): 过去的方法主要依赖于如Spitzer和WISE等望远镜，它们在高红移（z > 1）的分辨率不足，无法有效观察被尘埃遮蔽的星系。本文提出的方法使用了James Webb Space Telescope (JWST)上的MIRI，拥有更高分辨率，能够观察到z∼3的被遮蔽星系，从而解决了上述问题。该方法很好地满足了所需的观测条件。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于介绍了MEGA调查，提供了EGS领域的高质量MIRI成像，并填补了CEERS NIRCam观测的空白，为研究被遮蔽的宇宙提供了重要数据。

- (4): 本文提出的研究方法包括对MEGA调查的观测设置、数据减缩的过程，以及光度目录的创建，同时介绍了数据质量评估的步骤。

- (5): 本文在四个波段上提供了新的星系数量计数，显示了MEGA调查的数据深度和覆盖度。这些表现支持了对星系演化和活动星系核的科学目标的追求。


## DESI DR2 Results II: Measurements of Baryon Acoustic Oscillations and Cosmological Constraints
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.14738v2
- **Authors**: ['DESI Collaboration', 'M. Abdul Karim', 'J. Aguilar', 'S. Ahlen', 'S. Alam', 'L. Allen', 'C. Allende Prieto', 'O. Alves', 'A. Anand', 'U. Andrade', 'E. Armengaud', 'A. Aviles', 'S. Gaztañaga', 'H. Gil-Marín', 'S. Gontcho A Gontcho', 'D. Gonzalez', 'A. X. Gonzalez-Morales', 'C. Gordon', 'D. Green', 'G. Gutierrez', 'J. Guy', 'B. Hadzhiyska', 'C. Hahn', 'S. He', 'M. Herbold', 'H.
